**Summary of `README.md`**  
The README introduces **Consoul**, an AIpowered terminal assistant that supports multiple AI providers (Claude, GPT4, Gemini, local models). It offers a rich TUI via Textual, a simple CLI, and an SDK for programmatic use. Key features include:

- Interactive conversations with streaming responses and history.
- File editing, code search, and image analysis tools.
- Multiprovider and localmodel support.
- Security controls: permission policies, approval workflows, audit logs.
- Comprehensive documentation and configuration guide.

The project is opensource under the MIT license, with clear contributing guidelines and CI/test coverage.
